# Datastore Schema - Agent Studio Source And Route Ledger

## Purpose

This note converts the LLM Engineers Handbook canon decisions into concrete Agent Studio datastore objects. It is not an implementation migration. It is the source-aware schema contract that future migrations, APIs, and agent traces should preserve.

## Design Rules

- Store source identity and provenance before any extraction, chunking, embedding, note synthesis, or generation.
- Treat raw sources, extracted artifacts, chunks, embeddings, Obsidian notes, eval datasets, and route releases as different object types.
- Keep raw book/source text out of notes and ordinary traces; store references, hashes, compact summaries, and evidence IDs.
- Bind prompts, graph definitions, model routes, retrieval snapshots, eval suites, guardrails, and serving profiles into explicit releases.
- Preserve rejected evidence and rejected outputs, because they are needed for retrieval tuning and preference alignment.

## Core Objects

| Object | Primary job | Key fields |
|---|---|---|
| `source_record` | Canonical source identity and rights/provenance record | `source_id`, `source_class`, `path_or_url`, `title`, `authors`, `publisher_or_owner`, `rights_status`, `provenance_status`, `official_source_url`, `local_hash`, `metadata_hash`, `discovered_at`, `source_adapter`, `status` |
| `web_source_candidate` | Candidate web URL before fetch or extraction | `candidate_id`, `discovered_url`, `discovery_source_ref`, `anchor_or_listing_context`, `source_owner`, `expected_source_class`, `discovered_at`, `status` |
| `robots_policy_check` | Crawl-policy evidence for one URL, scope, and user agent | `robots_check_id`, `candidate_id`, `robots_url`, `user_agent`, `scope_host_protocol_port`, `fetch_status`, `matched_rule`, `allowed_to_fetch`, `checked_at`, `cache_until`, `error_policy` |
| `web_fetch_record` | HTTP fetch, redirect, content, and cache-validator evidence | `fetch_id`, `candidate_id`, `requested_url`, `final_url`, `redirect_chain_hash`, `status_code`, `content_type`, `content_length`, `etag`, `last_modified`, `response_hash`, `fetched_at` |
| `canonical_url_record` | Duplicate/canonical mapping without losing observed provenance | `canonical_record_id`, `observed_url`, `canonical_url`, `canonical_method`, `sitemap_ref`, `confidence`, `conflict_notes`, `created_at` |
| `sitemap_discovery_record` | Sitemap/feed discovery and freshness hint record | `sitemap_record_id`, `sitemap_url`, `format`, `parent_scope`, `url_count`, `lastmod_policy`, `discovered_url_refs`, `fetched_at`, `status` |
| `source_terms_review` | Rights, license, and product-use review separate from crawl allowance | `terms_review_id`, `source_ref`, `terms_url`, `license_or_terms_summary`, `allowed_uses`, `blocked_uses`, `reviewer`, `reviewed_at`, `status` |
| `web_source_refresh_policy` | Freshness and recrawl policy for a web source | `refresh_policy_id`, `source_ref`, `freshness_signal_refs`, `refresh_cadence`, `stale_after`, `change_detection_method`, `owner`, `status` |
| `source_freshness_observation` | Signal that a source or source policy may have changed | `observation_id`, `source_ref`, `signal_type`, `signal_value_hash`, `observed_at`, `observer`, `confidence`, `recommended_action` |
| `source_dependency_edge` | Dependency from a source snapshot to a derived note, chunk, embedding, claim, eval, approval, cache, route card, or artifact | `edge_id`, `source_snapshot_ref`, `derived_object_ref`, `derived_object_type`, `dependency_type`, `created_by_run_ref`, `status` |
| `source_invalidation_event` | Stale/blocking event after source, rights, extraction, retrieval, cache, policy, or route change | `invalidation_id`, `source_ref`, `change_class`, `affected_object_refs`, `stale_reason`, `required_refresh_refs`, `review_required`, `created_at`, `status` |
| `source_refresh_diff` | Comparison between old and new source-derived evidence | `diff_id`, `old_snapshot_ref`, `new_snapshot_ref`, `content_hash_delta`, `claim_delta_refs`, `retrieval_metric_delta_refs`, `rights_delta`, `decision` |
| `stale_artifact_review` | Review decision for an artifact affected by stale source evidence | `review_id`, `artifact_ref`, `invalidation_ref`, `support_state_before`, `support_state_after`, `publish_or_route_impact`, `decision`, `reviewed_at` |
| `source_freshness_invalidation_release_gate` | Promotion gate for source refresh, index refresh, parser change, rights change, cache-policy change, or source-backed route release | `gate_id`, `route_id`, `candidate_release_id`, `freshness_observation_refs`, `source_snapshot_refs`, `rights_provenance_refs`, `dependency_edge_refs`, `invalidation_event_refs`, `refresh_diff_refs`, `rebuilt_projection_refs`, `claim_ledger_refs`, `cache_invalidation_refs`, `eval_rerun_refs`, `stale_artifact_review_refs`, `rollback_or_correction_ref`, `decision`, `reviewed_at` |
| `bulk_crawl_snapshot_ref` | Common Crawl or other bulk web-corpus snapshot reference | `snapshot_ref_id`, `corpus_provider`, `crawl_id`, `index_ref`, `record_locator`, `capture_time`, `warc_or_extract_class`, `terms_review_ref`, `status` |
| `web_source_acquisition_release_gate` | Promotion gate before a fetched web source can become retrieval/canon evidence | `gate_id`, `candidate_id`, `robots_policy_check_ref`, `web_fetch_record_ref`, `canonical_url_record_ref`, `sitemap_discovery_ref`, `source_terms_review_ref`, `extraction_quality_ref`, `privacy_or_pii_review_ref`, `refresh_policy_ref`, `bulk_snapshot_ref`, `decision`, `reviewer`, `reviewed_at` |
| `crawl_projection_record` | Raw archive, metadata, or extracted-text projection of a crawled source | `projection_id`, `source_ref`, `projection_type`, `crawl_id`, `record_locator`, `url`, `http_metadata_ref`, `created_at`, `status` |
| `source_sample_inspection` | Inspection evidence before a source adapter or filter policy is trusted | `inspection_id`, `source_snapshot_ref`, `sample_method`, `sample_count`, `quality_findings`, `risk_findings`, `recommended_filter_changes`, `reviewer`, `created_at` |
| `language_filter_result` | Language classifier decision and calibration signal | `result_id`, `artifact_ref`, `model_ref`, `predicted_language`, `confidence`, `threshold`, `manual_label_ref`, `decision`, `created_at` |
| `pii_masking_event` | PII detection and masking action over a source artifact | `masking_event_id`, `artifact_ref`, `policy_ref`, `pii_types`, `match_counts`, `masked_artifact_ref`, `false_positive_sample_refs`, `false_negative_review_ref`, `created_at` |
| `content_filter_result` | Harm, toxicity, NSFW, or safety classifier/rule result | `filter_result_id`, `artifact_ref`, `category`, `model_or_rule_ref`, `score`, `threshold`, `decision`, `calibration_sample_ref`, `created_at` |
| `quality_filter_result` | Deterministic or classifier-based quality decision | `quality_result_id`, `artifact_ref`, `filter_family`, `features_or_score_ref`, `threshold`, `decision`, `target_route_or_eval`, `rejection_reason`, `created_at` |
| `dedupe_cluster_record` | Exact or fuzzy duplicate cluster with retained provenance | `cluster_id`, `method`, `normalization_policy`, `hash_or_signature_refs`, `candidate_refs`, `similarity_threshold`, `retained_ref`, `removed_refs`, `false_merge_review` |
| `filter_stage_counter` | Kept, rejected, and modified counts for an ingestion stage | `counter_id`, `run_id`, `stage_name`, `input_count`, `kept_count`, `rejected_count`, `modified_count`, `top_rejection_reasons`, `sample_refs` |
| `validation_leakage_check` | Evidence that validation/eval material did not enter train/retrieval data | `check_id`, `candidate_dataset_ref`, `validation_dataset_ref`, `method`, `overlap_count`, `blocked_refs`, `review_status`, `created_at` |
| `tokenization_artifact_record` | Versioned tokenized projection of source text | `tokenization_id`, `source_dataset_ref`, `tokenizer_ref`, `eos_policy`, `dtype`, `document_boundary_policy`, `token_count`, `output_artifact_ref`, `created_at` |
| `pipeline_runtime_benchmark` | Runtime, throughput, and cost evidence for source processing | `benchmark_id`, `run_id`, `input_size`, `worker_count`, `hardware_or_service_ref`, `elapsed_time`, `throughput`, `cost_estimate`, `bottleneck_notes` |
| `source_filter_pipeline_release_gate` | Promotion gate before source filtering, dedupe, tokenization, embedding, or eval-data generation affects retrieval, tuning, evals, or canon notes | `gate_id`, `pipeline_release_id`, `candidate_source_snapshot_ref`, `crawl_projection_refs`, `source_sample_inspection_refs`, `language_filter_refs`, `pii_masking_refs`, `content_filter_refs`, `quality_filter_refs`, `dedupe_cluster_refs`, `filter_stage_counter_refs`, `validation_leakage_check_refs`, `tokenization_artifact_refs`, `embedding_artifact_refs`, `accepted_sample_refs`, `rejected_sample_refs`, `bias_false_negative_review_refs`, `pipeline_runtime_benchmark_refs`, `rollback_snapshot_ref`, `decision`, `reviewed_at` |
| `ingestion_run` | Auditable execution record for source intake or refresh | `run_id`, `started_at`, `finished_at`, `operator`, `adapter_version`, `input_scope`, `attempted_count`, `success_count`, `skipped_count`, `failed_count`, `failure_reasons`, `output_artifact_ids` |
| `note_artifact` | Human-readable synthesis note derived from source work | `note_artifact_id`, `path`, `source_ids`, `run_id`, `note_type`, `coverage_status_id`, `stores_raw_text`, `stores_long_excerpts`, `status`, `updated_at` |
| `coverage_status` | Promotion state for a source, URL, chapter, video, or note | `coverage_status_id`, `subject_ref`, `subject_type`, `status`, `evidence_note_ids`, `cross_check_refs`, `recommended_next_action`, `updated_at` |
| `decision_reference` | Source-backed link from an architecture decision to evidence | `decision_reference_id`, `decision_ref`, `source_ids`, `note_artifact_ids`, `confidence`, `assumption_flags`, `tie_breaker_needed`, `created_at` |
| `audit_record` | Daily or weekly ingestion/vault-map maintenance record | `audit_id`, `audit_type`, `scope`, `source_delta_count`, `coverage_delta`, `map_changes`, `blockers`, `recommended_next_actions`, `created_at` |
| `object_artifact_release_gate` | Promotion gate proving binary evidence is replayable, retained, and access-audited | `gate_id`, `artifact_id`, `release_ref`, `object_ref_id`, `storage_policy_ref`, `object_version_event_refs`, `object_lifecycle_event_refs`, `signed_access_event_refs`, `restore_drill_refs`, `dependent_route_eval_publication_refs`, `decision`, `reviewer`, `created_at` |
| `artifact_object_ref` | Binary object pointer for source files, generated artifacts, sandbox exports, manifests, eval outputs, or note attachments | `object_ref_id`, `artifact_id`, `provider`, `bucket_or_container`, `object_key`, `version_or_generation`, `content_hash`, `size_bytes`, `mime_type`, `encryption_profile`, `created_at`, `status` |
| `object_storage_policy` | Bucket/container-level storage contract by artifact class | `policy_id`, `provider`, `bucket_or_container`, `artifact_classes`, `versioning_enabled`, `immutability_or_lock_mode`, `retention_period`, `lifecycle_rule_refs`, `replication_policy`, `access_logging`, `review_status` |
| `object_version_event` | Upload, overwrite, delete-marker, restore, or version promotion evidence | `event_id`, `object_ref_id`, `event_type`, `previous_version_ref`, `new_version_or_generation`, `producer_run_id`, `request_hash`, `integrity_check`, `created_at` |
| `object_lifecycle_event` | Tier movement, expiration, retention change, hold, or restore-state transition | `lifecycle_event_id`, `object_ref_id`, `policy_id`, `event_type`, `storage_class_or_tier`, `effective_at`, `restore_by`, `replay_impact`, `review_status` |
| `signed_object_access_event` | Temporary delegated object access through signed URL, SAS, or provider equivalent | `access_event_id`, `object_ref_id`, `issuer_ref`, `recipient_surface`, `allowed_operations`, `expiry`, `credential_type`, `scope_hash`, `revocation_posture`, `created_at` |
| `object_restore_drill` | Evidence that archived or retained artifact classes can be restored for audit/replay | `drill_id`, `policy_id`, `artifact_class`, `sample_object_refs`, `requested_at`, `available_at`, `restore_latency`, `integrity_result`, `decision` |
| `question_backlog_item` | Non-canon question or concept coverage item | `question_id`, `source_id`, `cluster`, `question_hash`, `target_route_surface`, `target_eval_surface`, `priority`, `canon_check_status`, `created_at` |
| `concept_coverage_record` | Link from a concept to canon evidence and eval gaps | `concept_id`, `concept_name`, `canon_note_refs`, `eval_case_refs`, `unresolved_gap`, `risk_level`, `owner`, `updated_at` |
| `learning_eval_case` | Eval for source-backed concept explanation | `case_id`, `concept_id`, `route_id`, `prompt_ref`, `required_source_refs`, `expected_behavior`, `forbidden_behavior`, `grader_policy`, `status` |
| `answer_canon_check` | Verification that an answer is supported by canon notes | `check_id`, `artifact_id`, `question_id`, `canon_source_refs`, `unsupported_claim_flags`, `private_source_used_as_evidence`, `review_status`, `created_at` |
| `stakeholder_requirement_record` | Route requirement tied to affected stakeholders and constraints | `requirement_id`, `route_id`, `stakeholder_type`, `objective`, `constraint_refs`, `success_metric_refs`, `harm_or_failure_cost`, `reviewer_capacity_assumption`, `owner`, `status` |
| `governance_release_gate` | Non-accuracy release gate for a route | `gate_id`, `route_release_id`, `stakeholder_requirement_refs`, `required_dimensions`, `success_metric_refs`, `fairness_slice_eval_refs`, `label_caveat_refs`, `model_design_tradeoff_refs`, `business_value_metric_refs`, `human_review_burden_refs`, `blocking_findings`, `approved_tradeoffs`, `incident_feedback_path_ref`, `rollback_target_ref`, `reviewer_refs`, `decision`, `reviewed_at` |
| `fairness_slice_eval` | Slice-level quality and harm evaluation | `slice_eval_id`, `route_id`, `eval_dataset_id`, `slice_definition`, `label_availability`, `metrics`, `intersectional_refs`, `proxy_feature_caveats`, `thresholds`, `decision_status` |
| `label_caveat_record` | Missing-label and annotation caveat for governance review | `label_caveat_id`, `source_or_eval_ref`, `sensitive_or_proxy_feature`, `label_status`, `annotation_disagreement`, `legal_or_consent_constraint`, `known_limitations`, `mitigation`, `owner` |
| `model_design_tradeoff_record` | Evidence for model/system optimization tradeoffs | `tradeoff_id`, `route_id`, `change_ref`, `optimized_dimension`, `expected_gain`, `affected_slices`, `measured_regressions`, `privacy_security_notes`, `rollback_policy`, `decision_status` |
| `business_value_metric` | Business or user-value metric linked to route decisions | `business_metric_id`, `route_id`, `stakeholder_requirement_id`, `metric_name`, `measurement_window`, `target`, `cost_of_error`, `reviewer_capacity_limit`, `rollout_decision_ref` |
| `source_datasheet_record` | Dataset/source documentation for governed reuse | `datasheet_id`, `source_or_dataset_ref`, `owner`, `motivation`, `composition_summary`, `acquisition_path`, `rights_status`, `transform_refs`, `excluded_material`, `known_gaps`, `freshness_policy`, `recommended_uses`, `prohibited_uses`, `review_status`, `updated_at` |
| `model_provider_card_record` | Model or provider documentation for governed runtime use | `model_provider_card_id`, `model_or_provider_ref`, `version_ref`, `license_or_access_terms`, `intended_use`, `unsupported_use`, `limitations`, `evaluation_slice_refs`, `safety_notes`, `training_or_data_disclosure_refs`, `data_boundary_refs`, `allowed_product_surfaces`, `review_status`, `updated_at` |
| `route_card_record` | Searchable model/route card for governed AI systems | `route_card_id`, `route_id`, `owner`, `purpose`, `supported_uses`, `unsupported_uses`, `model_or_provider_refs`, `source_datasheet_refs`, `eval_slice_refs`, `deployment_status`, `metric_refs`, `risk_refs`, `fallback_ref`, `rollback_ref`, `explainability_refs`, `supporting_docs`, `governance_status`, `updated_at` |
| `risk_register_entry` | NIST-style risk record tied to route, source, model/provider, or artifact releases | `risk_id`, `risk_family`, `affected_subject_refs`, `likelihood`, `impact`, `harm_or_failure_mode`, `control_refs`, `measurement_signal_refs`, `owner`, `review_cadence`, `escalation_path`, `fallback_ref`, `status`, `updated_at` |

| `vision_language_grounding_release_gate` | Promotion gate before captioning, VQA, alt text, image-text retrieval, OCR/question answering, or visual source-claim routes affect product evidence | `gate_id`, `route_id`, `candidate_release_id`, `vision_language_task_ref`, `input_artifact_refs`, `source_snapshot_ref`, `question_or_prompt_ref`, `expected_answer_type`, `allowed_inference_level`, `risk_level`, `visible_evidence_refs`, `region_or_mask_refs`, `frame_or_object_track_refs`, `visual_claim_refs`, `caption_artifact_refs`, `unsupported_claim_flags`, `vqa_trace_refs`, `cross_modal_retrieval_trace_refs`, `source_evidence_refs`, `forbidden_inference_policy_ref`, `cross_modal_grounding_eval_refs`, `wrong_region_eval_refs`, `unsupported_caption_eval_refs`, `prompt_sensitivity_eval_refs`, `ocr_text_eval_refs`, `counting_spatial_eval_refs`, `source_conflict_eval_refs`, `fallback_route_ref`, `rollback_target_ref`, `incident_feedback_path_ref`, `decision`, `reviewed_at` |
| `stale_dependency_record` | Staleness created by source/artifact/route changes | `stale_dependency_id`, `changed_ref`, `dependent_refs`, `stale_reason`, `required_refresh`, `owner`, `status`, `created_at` |

## Source Record Requirements

Every source record must answer:

- What is the source?
- Where did it come from?
- Why is it legal/in scope?
- Which adapter read it?
- Which extraction run produced downstream artifacts?
- Which notes, chunks, evals, or generated outputs depend on it?

Required source classes:

- `local_book_pdf`
- `local_docx`
- `local_image`
- `official_doc_page`
- `official_whitepaper`
- `official_course_page`
- `official_video_listing`
- `official_github_repo`
- `open_research_paper`
- `generated_note`
- `feedback_artifact`

## Retrieval Trace Requirements

Retrieval traces must keep both accepted and rejected evidence:

- accepted evidence supports the final answer;
- rejected evidence shows what the system considered but excluded;
- rejected reasons help tune metadata filters, rerankers, query rewrites, and graph traversal;
- missing evidence should create eval and ingestion backlog items.

The trace should store content references and compact reason summaries, not raw book excerpts.

Graph-aware retrieval traces also need:

- retrieval mode: local graph, global/community, DRIFT-style, NL-to-graph query, lexical, vector, or hybrid;
- graph start nodes;
- allowed edge types;
- traversal depth;
- community report IDs considered;
- community reports rejected;
- graph query text or structured query object when applicable;
- graph traversal latency and graph result count.

## Preference Pair Requirements

Preference alignment data must be contrastive and provenance-aware:

- store the chosen output and rejected output by artifact ID;
- record whether the evaluator was the user, an editor, a reviewer agent, or a model judge;
- record the rubric and candidate order;
- attach source evidence when the preference involves grounding;
- separate human-ranked, model-ranked, and synthetic pairs.

Preference pairs are for behavior/style/alignment tuning. They are not a source of factual truth.

## Serving Profile Requirements

Every route must declare a serving profile before production use:

- `realtime_interrupt` for barge-in and fast voice turns;
- `conversational_reply` for streamed dialogue;
- `quick_critique` for short agent review;
- `long_synthesis` for source-backed drafts;
- `background_research` for search/retrieval expansion;
- `batch_ingestion` for extraction, embedding refresh, and offline evals;
- `media_generation` for image/audio/video generation.

Deployment mode should be selected from:

- `real_time`
- `async_queue`
- `batch_transform`
- `local_job`
- `managed_api`

## Promotion Gates

A route can become an `agent_release` only when:

- agentic routes declare why model-controlled workflow execution is required, or the route is explicitly marked non-agentic;
- source and retrieval dependencies are versioned;
- prompt/model/graph versions are fixed;
- workflow graph edges are typed with schemas, trust class, and failure policy;
- tool contracts declare side-effect class, credential scope, and approval requirement;
- MCP servers expose only reviewed tools, resources, and prompts, with capability snapshots, auth grants, timeout policy, list-change drift handling, and output validation attached;
- security scope, tool permissions, input safety scans, and risk register entries are attached for routes that touch private data, untrusted inputs, external tools, or generated public artifacts;
- trust boundaries and trace redaction policy are attached for routes that use retrieval, uploads, browser/computer-use, or external tools;
- security eval cases cover prompt injection, overprivileged tools, unauthorized retrieval, sensitive trace leakage, and content provenance for applicable surfaces;
- visual and multimodal routes attach media source records, visual/video traces, visual eval cases, and media generation records before public use;
- generated-media and audio routes attach model cards, media pipeline traces, control records, media adaptation records, audio representation records, consent records where applicable, local runtime profiles, and watermark/provenance records before public use;
- route change proposal is approved when the change affects production or canon-impacting workflows;
- route success contract is attached with explicit thresholds and blocked tradeoffs;
- decision policy and uncertainty-signal logging are attached when a route can answer, abstain, escalate, retrieve more, publish, or call side-effecting tools;
- eval suite and latest eval run are attached;
- baseline/candidate eval comparison is attached for prompt, model, graph, tool, retrieval, or guardrail changes;
- trace-grade coverage exists for graph, tool, handoff, or guardrail changes;
- tokenizer profile, context assembly trace policy, decoding policy, and reasoning trace coverage are attached for language-generation routes;
- task-pipeline, QA-pipeline, tokenization-eval, generated-text-metric, few-label-strategy, deployment-benchmark, compression, or pretraining records are attached when those route surfaces are used;
- approximate-inference, posterior-approximation, distribution-shift, interpretability-review, diversity-selection, and graph-structure records are attached when route decisions depend on inferred confidence, shift robustness, explanations, or graph structure;
- adaptation candidates are reviewed before PEFT, fine-tuning, distillation, or self-hosting work starts;
- alignment datasets, reward signals, and alignment runs have provenance, rights status, eval gates, and rollback before they can change a route;
- agentic routes declare agent environment and governed skill records when procedural memory is used;
- model routes attach architecture profiles and workload-slice measurements before serving-profile promotion;
- capacity estimates are attached before fine-tuning, PEFT, distillation, long-context adaptation, self-hosting, or model-provider migration;
- multilingual/public content routes attach language coverage slices and token-cost estimates;
- serving profile is attached;
- guardrail policy is attached;
- rollback route exists;
- content provenance exists before publishing generated social/media artifacts;
- publish destination records and approval edges exist before external media publication;
- incident feedback can create or update release-blocking eval cases;
- human approval is recorded for publishing or canon-impacting workflows.

## Failure Modes This Schema Prevents

- Source notes cannot be traced back to legal/provenance records.
- Vector chunks outlive deleted or blocked source material.
- Generated artifacts cannot explain which evidence was accepted or rejected.
- Fine-tuning data mixes synthetic, human, and source-derived examples without labels.
- Preference learning keeps winners but discards losers.
- A prompt update ships without matching eval, route, serving, and rollback metadata.
- Interactive and batch workloads share one unbounded serving path.

## Next Implementation Notes

- Translate this schema into Postgres tables with pgvector-backed retrieval tables.
- Add Obsidian note templates for `source_record`, `eval_dataset`, `preference_pair`, and `serving_profile`.
- Backfill existing vault source notes into `source_record`-shaped manifests before building ingestion automation. Current backfills: `05-ingestion-runs/source-records-official-open-backfill.json`, `05-ingestion-runs/source-records-local-books-backfill.json`, and `05-ingestion-runs/source-records-local-book-chapters-backfill.json`.
